Activity Types â€” Complete List
Seating & Table
ActivityIconLogged WhenTable seatedğŸ‘¥Guest seated (host or QR scan)Guest count updatedğŸ‘¥Waiter changes guest countTable changedğŸ”„Guest moved to different tableTables mergedğŸ”—Multiple tables combinedTables unmergedğŸ”“Merged tables separatedTable vacatedğŸšªGuest left (payment complete)Cleaning startedğŸ§¹Busser starts cleaningCleaning doneâœ…Table ready for next guest

Orders
ActivityIconLogged WhenOrder placedğŸ“Guest submits order (QR or waiter)Order modifiedâœï¸Item added/removed before kitchenCancel requestedâŒGuest requests cancellationCancel approvedâœ…Waiter approves cancelCancel rejectedâ›”Waiter rejects cancelItem unavailable markedğŸš«Kitchen marks item unavailableItem available markedâœ…Kitchen marks item available

Kitchen & Bar
ActivityIconLogged WhenOrder received (Kitchen)ğŸ“¥Kitchen display shows orderPrep startedğŸ³Cook taps "Start"Item readyâœ…Cook taps "Ready"Order received (Bar)ğŸ“¥Bar display shows orderDrink startedğŸ¹Bartender taps "Start"Drink readyâœ…Bartender taps "Ready"

Waiter Actions
ActivityIconLogged WhenWater servedğŸ’§Waiter taps "Water Served"Food picked upğŸ½ï¸Waiter picks from kitchenFood servedğŸ½ï¸Waiter delivers to tableDrink picked upğŸ¹Waiter picks from barDrink servedğŸ¹Waiter delivers to tableAssistance acknowledgedğŸ™‹Waiter taps "On My Way"Assistance completedâœ…Waiter completes request

Billing & Payment
ActivityIconLogged WhenBill requestedğŸ§¾Guest requests billBill printedğŸ–¨ï¸Staff prints billBill deliveredğŸ§¾Waiter delivers billPayment collectedğŸ’µCash/card collectedPayment completedâœ…Full payment donePartial paymentğŸ’³Part of bill paid

Manager Actions
ActivityIconLogged WhenDiscount appliedğŸ’°Manager adds discountItem voidedâŒManager voids itemItem replacedğŸ”„Manager sends replacementWaiter reassignedğŸ‘¤Manager changes waiterNote addedğŸ“Manager adds internal note

Staff & Shift
ActivityIconLogged WhenShift startedâ–¶ï¸Staff clocks inShift endedâ¹ï¸Staff clocks outBreak startedâ¸ï¸Staff takes breakBreak endedâ–¶ï¸Staff returns from breakTable assignedğŸ“‹Table assigned to waiter

Issues & Escalations
ActivityIconLogged WhenAssistance requestedğŸ™‹Guest calls waiterFood issue reportedâš ï¸Guest reports problemEscalation triggeredğŸ”´System auto-escalatesIssue resolvedâœ…Staff resolves issue

Activity Log Entry â€” Data Structure
ActivityLog {
  id
  timestamp: datetime (precise to second)

  // What happened
  activity_type: string
  activity_category: "seating" | "order" | "kitchen" | "bar" |
                     "waiter" | "billing" | "manager" | "staff" | "issue"

  // Where
  table_id (optional)
  session_id (optional)
  order_id (optional)
  item_id (optional)

  // Who
  performed_by: staff_id | "guest" | "system"
  staff_name: string
  staff_role: string

  // Details
  description: string
  details: JSON {
    // varies by activity type
  }

  // Priority
  priority: "critical" | "urgent" | "warning" | "info" | "notice"

  // For time-based metrics
  related_activity_id (optional) // links start â†’ end events
}

Example Log Entries
Table Seated
json{
  "timestamp": "2026-01-23T15:27:15.342Z",
  "activity_type": "table_seated",
  "activity_category": "seating",
  "table_id": 7,
  "session_id": 501,
  "performed_by": "staff_12",
  "staff_name": "Sita",
  "staff_role": "Host",
  "description": "Table 7 seated with 4 guests",
  "details": {
    "guest_count": 4,
    "seating_method": "host_assigned"
  },
  "priority": "info"
}
Food Issue Reported
json{
  "timestamp": "2026-01-23T15:30:58.127Z",
  "activity_type": "food_issue_reported",
  "activity_category": "issue",
  "table_id": 5,
  "session_id": 498,
  "order_id": 1247,
  "item_id": 3421,
  "performed_by": "guest",
  "staff_name": null,
  "staff_role": null,
  "description": "Food issue reported: Rice is cold",
  "details": {
    "issue_type": "quality",
    "item_name": "Fried Rice",
    "guest_note": "Rice is cold"
  },
  "priority": "urgent"
}
Discount Applied
json{
  "timestamp": "2026-01-23T15:30:12.891Z",
  "activity_type": "discount_applied",
  "activity_category": "manager",
  "table_id": 3,
  "session_id": 495,
  "performed_by": "staff_1",
  "staff_name": "Admin",
  "staff_role": "Manager",
  "description": "Discount Rs. 200 applied to Table 3",
  "details": {
    "discount_type": "fixed",
    "discount_amount": 200,
    "original_bill": 1450,
    "new_bill": 1250,
    "reason": "Compensation for cold food"
  },
  "priority": "notice"
}

Order Progress Tracking â€” The Concept
Order has 3 items, total quantity 4:

2x Chicken Momo
1x Fried Rice
1x Dal

Log should show progress as fraction:

1/4 â€” first Momo ready
2/4 â€” second Momo ready
3/4 â€” Fried Rice ready
4/4 â€” Dal ready (order complete)

Table Session â€” Complete Lifecycle
A session starts when guest sits and ends when table is cleaned and ready.

Session Data Structure
TableSession {
  id: "session_501"
  table_id: 5
  table_ids: [5]  // multiple if merged
  is_merged: false

  // Guest info
  guest_count: 4
  guest_count_history: [
    { count: 4, changed_by: "host", at: "2:45 PM" },
    { count: 6, changed_by: "waiter_ram", reason: "2 joined", at: "3:10 PM" }
  ]

  host_id: "staff_12"
  waiter_id: "staff_5"
  waiter_history: [
    { waiter_id: "staff_5", assigned_at: "2:45 PM" },
    { waiter_id: "staff_8", assigned_at: "3:30 PM", reason: "shift change" }
  ]

  first_food_served_at: "3:08:02 PM"

  vacated_at: "4:08:31 PM"

  cleaning_completed_at: "4:13:00 PM"
  session_ended_at: "4:13:00 PM"

  // Status
  status: "completed"  // active | billing | vacated | cleaning | completed

  // Orders
  orders: [
    { order_id: 1253, placed_at: "2:52 PM", items: 4, status: "served" },
    { order_id: 1267, placed_at: "3:45 PM", items: 2, status: "served" }
  ]
  total_items_ordered: 6
  total_items_served: 6

  // Assistance
  assistance_requests: [
    { type: "water_refill", requested_at: "3:15 PM", completed_at: "3:17 PM" },
    { type: "food_issue", requested_at: "3:30 PM", completed_at: "3:35 PM", note: "cold rice" }
  ]

  // Billing

  discount_applied: 200

    { method: "cash", amount: 500 },
    { method: "card", amount: 1150 }
  ]

    { type: "food_issue", item: "Fried Rice", note: "cold", resolved: true }
  ]

  // Manager actions

    { type: "discount", amount: 200, by: "admin", at: "3:32 PM" }
  ]

    total_duration: "1h 28m",
    water_service_time: "3m 18s",
    avg_food_wait_time: "15m 47s",
    avg_assistance_response: "1m 30s",
    bill_wait_time: "1m 15s",
    cleaning_time: "4m"
  }
}
